<div id="review_1467295141" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1467295141" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1467295141?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=family-aspect">family-aspect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=kids-baby">kids-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe">safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=military-security-government">military-security-government</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1467295141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17009701807387340083"><b>4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 9/12/2016)</i></b><br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 3/18/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was a lot better than I thought it'd be! I had written it off before, because lots of readers didn't like the fact that Chace slept around while Faye was crushing on him. While I understand where they're coming from, it really didn't bother me. I still felt like Faye was a strong character, and she never crossed that line into doormat status for me (which is what I was really worried about). To clarify -- we d</span>
  <span id="freeText17009701807387340083" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 9/12/2016)</i></b><br /><br /><b>3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 3/18/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was a lot better than I thought it'd be! I had written it off before, because lots of readers didn't like the fact that Chace slept around while Faye was crushing on him. While I understand where they're coming from, it really didn't bother me. I still felt like Faye was a strong character, and she never crossed that line into doormat status for me (which is what I was really worried about). To clarify -- we don't experience any this sleeping around happening, but it is mentioned towards the beginning. I was not expecting the side story with the kid at all. I really loved how they worked to get him help, and how we got to see him in the epilogue as a happy young man! It was fun to see all of our Carnal (and Gnaw Bone) characters again, and it just makes me want to read about them all over again. I just LOVED Faye! She has to be one of my absolute favorite KA heroines! I am so happy that I followed my gut and gave this one a shot, because if I didn't I'd miss out on Faye ;)<br /><br /><b>Re-Read Update:</b> I got a little bored this time reading it if I'm completely honest. I didn't remember everything but I remembered a lot, so that might've contributed to my lack of attention to the story. I didn't, however, skim and I got all the way through it. It could be all the distractions going on and the craziness of the world right now that contributed to it too. Otherwise I still really liked Faye, liked the side character's roles in this, and liked the side story with the kid. <br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Faye and Chace's story. Chace's is still struggling with his guilt over his wife's murder (that happened in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12958487.Lady_Luck__Colorado_Mountain___3_" title="Lady Luck (Colorado Mountain, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Luck</a>), so when he bumps into Faye he isn't expecting it. Faye has been crushing hard on Chace for many years. She knows that something wasn't right about his marriage but never knew the exact details <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he was blackmailed into marrying the OW <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, so she knows that he didn't care for his wife but needs some help in getting out of his guilt. So when she bumps into him a few times, she decides to take the leap and expose her attraction towards him. Faye finds out that there is a child that is stealing books from her library and looks as if he is severely malnourished and has been beaten, so she takes it to policeman Chace because she is concerned. They work together to try to help the boy, and end up getting together and falling in love. There is a good bit of drama left over from Chace's past, some sexy times, some sweet and sad moments...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Faye and Chace's POV. I really liked that we got Chace's pov at times, as not all KA books give us that!<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good for the most part. I never skimmed, but it did feel a little too long at times.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, but they had been crushing on each other for years.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Chace. I liked him. He was a typical KA alpha hero, so I'm not complaining! I appreciated that he listened to her and snapped out of his little funk (the 1 time he was ticking me off), and he acknowledged his mess up and apologized.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 5 stars. Faye. I had hesitated to read this one, because I had seen people saying that she is a doormat type h -- I didn't get that at all!! She was a total nerd, she was sweet, and she had a backbone! I loved her :)<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b> Low/moderate. The kid killed me! The only times I teared up were with the kid, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H pushes the h away at first because he is still messed it about the murder of his wife (the actual murder and not because he loved her). It doesn't last long, and once he snaps out of it he strongly pursues the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some hot chemistry and scenes, but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. Condoms are used until a birth control talk happens. I don't remember any mention of the H's past practices.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Mild <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H carries a lot of guilt about his wife being murdered, but it is mainly about how he didn't prevent it and not at all because he loved her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Homelessness, child neglect and physical abuse, mentions of rape and a few murders, kidnapping, widower H, and a virgin h.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had great closure with many jump ahead moments in a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid the $4.99 on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd say that this should be <u>Safe</u> for most readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away (minimal)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse of side character (child)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_748307092" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/748307092" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/748307092?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer748307092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18312037090397544022">♦ <b>4.5 JUST BREATHE STARS.</b> ♦<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382893014i/6262238._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Kristen Ashley</b> has done it again. Each time I've finished one of her books, I think I've found my new favorite and that the rest of them won't be able to live up to the ones I've read already; and (almost) each time I'm proven wrong. <b>Breathe</b> was different from most of her other books in the sense that the heroine was much different from most other KA heroines, and that's exactly why I loved this book so much. Other than that, the story consisted of the typical KA eleme</span>
  <span id="freeText18312037090397544022" style="display:none">♦ <b>4.5 JUST BREATHE STARS.</b> ♦<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382893014i/6262238._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kristen Ashley</b> has done it again. Each time I've finished one of her books, I think I've found my new favorite and that the rest of them won't be able to live up to the ones I've read already; and (almost) each time I'm proven wrong. <b>Breathe</b> was different from most of her other books in the sense that the heroine was much different from most other KA heroines, and that's exactly why I loved this book so much. Other than that, the story consisted of the typical KA elements to make it a memorable read: hot alpha male with a kind heart, action, suspense, a bit of heartbreak and a suggary sweet happy ending.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382893014i/6262239._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Faye Goodknight</b> is such a refreshing heroine. She's shy, introvert, kindhearted and a little nerdy (okay, maybe more than a little). She's the town's quiet, pretty librarian. She loves to read, listen to music and watch her favorite shows on TV. Ever since she first laid eyes on Chace Keaton when she was sixteen years old, she's been in love with him. But, with her being the shy person she is, she's never worked up the courage to approaching him. So, when he finally notices her and strikes up a conversation, it seems as if her "holding out for a hero" has finally paid off.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382893014i/6262240._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Chace Keaton</b> has had a rough couple of years. In order to keep his father's secrets safe from his mother, he had to sacrifice a lot in his life. He had to become a dirty cop and was forced to marry Misty, a woman he despises. Now, he's finally freed from his loveless marriage, but he's still determined to find out who killed his wife. At the same time, his father and his associates still pester him about turning back to becoming a dirty cop. So, with a lot of darkness in his past and current life, the presence of the town's sweet librarian (who he's had his eyes on for a long time) feels like a breath of fresh air; and he's determined to do whatever it takes to keep her in his life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You in my life, me livin' in hell, feels like I've been touched by an angel."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Their romance is slowbuilding, sweet and heartwarming. Chace is a genuinely "good man", who still possesses the right amount of KA alpha male hotness. At first he's kind of a jerk to Faye, but that's only because of his past and because of the fact that he doesn't want her to get hurt. Still, he proved his true kindness by taking care of Malachi and by doing anything in his power to make Faye breathe easily and make her happy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382894444i/6262813._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kristen Ashley's books have become my "go to"-comfort books. So far, I've never been disappointed with any of the one's I've read and although each series has it's perks, I think the Colorado Mountain series is one of my favorites. After the amazing previous books of the series, <i>Sweet Dreams</i> and <i>Lady Luck</i>, I wasn't sure <i>Breathe</i> would be able to live up to this two, and even though I still loved those slightly more, safe to say <i>Breathe</i> was a worthy follow-up!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382902812i/6266822._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'll take you thinking I'm your angel, but you need to know you're my hero."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="18312037090397544022" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1057749297" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057749297" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057749297?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057749297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1861580575656121447"><b>*** 4 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the most awesome book addicts at BB&B!!!</b><br/><br/>She did it again! And every time I finish one of her books I am still stumped as to how do books so over the top and full of flaws keep on stealing all my attention for hours at a time, completely oblivious to the world around me... It gets so bad that I forget all things real, forget about food or loved ones, (the food thing is actually a positive side effect!), and I even forget that I don't live in Colorado... These books are </span>
  <span id="freeText1861580575656121447" style="display:none"><b>*** 4 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the most awesome book addicts at BB&amp;B!!!</b><br /><br />She did it again! And every time I finish one of her books I am still stumped as to how do books so over the top and full of flaws keep on stealing all my attention for hours at a time, completely oblivious to the world around me... It gets so bad that I forget all things real, forget about food or loved ones, (the food thing is actually a positive side effect!), and I even forget that I don't live in Colorado... These books are so distracting, that we have to plan on times of the week void of other responsibilities so we don't screw them up... And it leaves me wander, what is it about KA that emersed us so fully in her stories???<br /><br />Magic. There is no other reasonable explanation. How can such crazy stories with crazy situations, crazier characters in insane relationships and most irrational happily ever afters, formulaic but lovable, make us so addicted and jonezing for the next hit otherwise???? Magic, no other explanation....<br /><br />In this book we are still in the mountains of Colorado and within the boundaries of the crooked police department which targeted Chase, his dad, his lait wife, and many more innocent people in the small town... This town has a small library and it has one full time employee - Faye, the redheaded, shy, introverted and sweet librarian. She has had a crush on the hero of taking down the corrupted Police Department, the brooding boy in blue, Chase, since she was 16. Her hopes had been diverted since Chase had gotten married 7 years ago, but close to an year ago he had lots his wife to a brutal murder and now Faye felt freer to watch and admire him, albeit from afar... But their first encounter is disastrous and the second convinces Faye Chase is not the Knight in shining armor she thought he was... <br /><br />Chase was a total jack ass and a big jerk to one of the sweetest, most beautiful women in the county, and definitely the purest of any he had met. Yes, his life in the last 10 years has been full of disasters, betrayals, he has been set up for a lifetime of misery, and it is only by chance that he finds himself free at the moment... A horrible, gruesome chance...<br /><br />As with all KA stories this is a romance. A crazy, making no sense at least in the beginning romance, a close to a caveman alpha with a woman who has issues romance, a "just because you know me your life will be in danger" type of romance, but I will promise you a happy ending kind of romance... We always have to suffer, put up with ridiculously pushy and dirty minded alphas, take kidnapping as a way to achieve a point for a given, and work through a multitude of spats and shootouts, all for the promise of that happy epilogue at the end. And it is worth it!!! Because she delivered on every point! <br /><br />I have to say that I absolutely fell in love with Faye - she lives in her books and loves all the geeky shows on TV! She had me at Firefly and Battle Star Galactica!!!! I would love to get in the middle of one of her tantrums when she invokes Darth Vader and the Skywalker relatives:-) Favorite parts of the book!!!<br /><br />The other favorite part, the side story of the two abused kids... Heartbreaking and inspiring at the same time... She had me ugly crying three times!!! That is just cruel!!!<br /><br />I will recommend this series to KA fans and those who like contemporary romance in a bit of a lower, earthier type of writing style... It is NOT perfect, it is NOT gentle, and at times, it is not pretty.. But I will be awaiting the next buddy read of her books with the craving of an addict... which I obviously have became.... More brains!¡!! Ops, wrong addiction, More books!!!! Happy reading, y'all!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1861580575656121447" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3562421645" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3562421645" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3562421645?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3562421645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5701554936252121045">#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3548182954?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Dreams</a> — 4.5 Stars<br/>#4 Breathe — 3.5 Stars<br/><br/><i>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_' title='Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Law Man</a>
</i> lookalike, but the combination in this was just not <i>right</i>. There was too much romance and not enough drama and suspense, which was what I loved about KA books. I think she developed and distributed those parts well. However, there was too much nothingness in <i>Breathe</i> that I really <i>felt</i> the book was too long.<br/><br/>I loved the part about Chace and Faye helping out Jeremiah and wanted more of it. The other parts about Misty’s murder and Chace’s </span>
  <span id="freeText5701554936252121045" style="display:none">#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3548182954?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a> — 4.5 Stars<br />#4 Breathe — 3.5 Stars<br /><br /><i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a>
</i> lookalike, but the combination in this was just not <i>right</i>. There was too much romance and not enough drama and suspense, which was what I loved about KA books. I think she developed and distributed those parts well. However, there was too much nothingness in <i>Breathe</i> that I really <i>felt</i> the book was too long.<br /><br />I loved the part about Chace and Faye helping out Jeremiah and wanted more of it. The other parts about Misty’s murder and Chace’s strained relationship with his father also didn’t get enough spotlight. I wanted to see both progression throughout the story but only got the resolution part of it in the last 20%.<br /><br />Chace wasn’t the “I want it, I’ll get it” type of guy, which was what I loved about KA Hs. They were always relentless in their pursuit. Macho alpha male as all get out but not like too forceful. Chace on the other hand was TOO controlling and bossy, and Faye was TOO agreeable. I suppose they fit each other, but they didn’t fit me.<br /><br />Do you understand what I’m saying? This was hard to explain. Idk guys, this time it was just different. There was no bitchy fights or crazy ex drama, and I missed those cause KA always gave them so good and fresh. This book falls flat compare to the other ones I’ve read so far, but it’s okay cause I still rounded it up to 4 stars (albeit begrudgingly). 🙈<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26402455-sana?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

<div id="review_1583626307" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1583626307" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1583626307?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9781455599110" href="/book/show/18773967-breathe">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1583626307" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6012860540927072527"><b>4 Faye You Fracking Saved this Book For Me Stars</b><br/><br/>Read with my KA-loving girls at <a>Buddies Books & Baubles</a><br/><br/><b>Faye Goodnight is one of the reasons I have a Chicks-I-Want-to-Hang-Out-With shelf. </b> She is everything I’m looking for in a Book BFF. Reasons I loved her from the beginning….<br/><br/>① - She always has her head in a book or nook. She loves to read and read to others.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Yes, I read. And yes, I do it a lot. And yes, I did it before you because life can suck and living in a fantasy world is a lot more fun</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6012860540927072527" style="display:none"><b>4 Faye You Fracking Saved this Book For Me Stars</b><br><br>Read with my KA-loving girls at <a>Buddies Books &amp; Baubles</a><br><br><b>Faye Goodnight is one of the reasons I have a Chicks-I-Want-to-Hang-Out-With shelf. </b> She is everything I’m looking for in a Book BFF. Reasons I loved her from the beginning….<br><br>① - She always has her head in a book or nook. She loves to read and read to others.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Yes, I read. And yes, I do it a lot. And yes, I did it before you because life can suck and living in a fantasy world is a lot more fun than living in the real world sometimes. This was not a weak choice, it was an informed one.”</i>
</blockquote><br>② - She has online friends that she chats with about different fandoms that they like and some of her real life bleeds into that.<br><br>③ - She watches some of the SCI-FI/Fantasy/Just Funny shows I love and will debate different aspects of them with you.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Feed me. If you don’t, all the way to Rosalinda’s, I’m explaining the entirety of the history of Angel, the vampire with a soul given to him by gypsies as punishment for him killing one of their own. This history will range from Buffy the Vampire Slayer through to Angel, his own TV show. I’ll also add my opinions on why they should never have cancelled Angel. I’ll tell you now, this is multi-part and doesn’t all have to do with the fact that David Boreanaz is hot. And, if you delay, I might even have time to get into why I think Joss Whedon should be recommended for sainthood.”</i>
</blockquote><br>④ - She swears using words from Battlestar Galactica….I LOVE IT!!! <i>airsick lowlanders (not from battlestar galactica but something I love to say when appropriate)</i><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The best television show fraking ever.”<br>I disagreed. I loved Battlestar Galactica but Firefly was by far and away the best television show ever, which made its midseason cancellation an act (I thought) of sacrilege. Fortunately, they made a movie about it. And also fortunately, Nathan Fillion moved on to another awesome show, Castle. <br>But nothing topped Firefly</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458759456i/18528024._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑤ - When she argues with you she loves to throw in various characters from Sci-Fi movies or books to help make her point.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“You know, even Darth Vader had the good grace to ask Luke to join him on the dark side.”</i>
</blockquote><br>So yeah Faye and I could totally hang out and be BFFs I’m sure of it. Chace on the other hand….*deep sigh* well he didn’t fare so well.<br><br>I normally read KA books for the uber alpha males that are great on paper, but seriously if my man said half of the stuff that they say to their women I would just giggle and walk the other way because who could take that seriously….#sorrynotsorry. But Chace is the first KA-alpha in forever that I just didn’t click with. I totally struggled with him as he kept digging his hole deeper and deeper and after Ty in the prior book being so awesome it was difficult to ever click with Chace. Really for the most part I tried to figure out why he deserved a girl as kickass as Faye totally was.<br><br>The rest of the story was pretty interesting though. Faye and Chace are trying to help a kid who looks like he keeps getting beat up and is probably underfed. As they try to work out who he is and how they can help him the story between the two of them starts to grow. The towns bad cops might be cleaned up but someone is still trying to pull a few strings in this small town and someone definitely wants those sex tapes that are being held in the town back and will go through some serious trouble to get them.<br><br>I like the storyline with Malachi (the kid they are trying to rescue) but I’m going to just say that KA went a smidgen over on the cheese factor there towards the end and I changed a little that she took it that far. But that said I did like most of the other stuff happening in the story.<br><br>As always there are some great side characters and we even get a cameo from one of the Rock Chicks…YAY. But Twyla by far stole the show for a minute when she was giving advice to our girl on how to let Chace know she was read for him to take her virginity (because yes of coarse she is a 29 year old virgin…because those are everywhere).<br><br><b>Recap:</b><br><br>Faye completely and totally awesome - ✔<br><br>Chace needs some help in the KA-Alpha department - ✔<br><br>Great side characters as always &amp; a cameo - ✔<br><br>Town I feel like I could live in - ✔<br><br>Set-up of our next potential Alpha male - ✔<br><br>Interesting plot line to supplement the romance - ✔<br><br>A KIDNAPPING (seriously wouldn’t be a KA book without at least one) - ✔<br><br><b>Standard Kristen Ashley Disclaimer</b>: I totally love her books but she is a love it or hate it author and so I almost never recommend her to friends and family for this reason. But I always fall into her stories and don’t come up for air until they are done….even though she breaks all the rules that I usually have for loving or hating a story and I still generally fall on the side of love.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6012860540927072527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1923334816" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14285971599858819342"><b>5 / 5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>reread:</b> <br/>23/05/17<br/>18/12/18<br/><br/><i>only five KA books past Bella? HUH, try eighteen in the past three months. I think I am addicted to Kristen Ashely's super dramatic and over-the-top series, a guilty pleasure that I can't seem to stop.</i><br/><br/>I'm a little late into reviewing this book as I have gone on to read three more from this series and two more from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> and adored them all. But in saying that, I feel like <i>Breathe</i> will forever be my favourite. <br/><br/>This a romance centered around Faye Goodkni</span>
  <span id="freeText14285971599858819342" style="display:none"><b>5 / 5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>reread:</b> <br />23/05/17<br />18/12/18<br /><br /><i>only five KA books past Bella? HUH, try eighteen in the past three months. I think I am addicted to Kristen Ashely's super dramatic and over-the-top series, a guilty pleasure that I can't seem to stop.</i><br /><br />I'm a little late into reviewing this book as I have gone on to read three more from this series and two more from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> and adored them all. But in saying that, I feel like <i>Breathe</i> will forever be my favourite. <br /><br />This a romance centered around Faye Goodknight who is as pure and kindhearted as her name suggests, the local librarian in a small town situated in Colorado <i>(where this whole particular series revolves)</i> with her head stuck permanently in a book. The only times she pops back into reality is to ogle and continue to crush on Detective Chace Keaton, a crush that has lasted thirteen years. <br /><br />They run into each other in the middle of the night when Faye is attempting to figure out the local murder mystery, the murder victim also being Chace's ex-wife, a woman who he had no affection for and let everybody know. <br /><br />Slowly, their relationship begins to bloom but Chace hasn't lived an all that charmed life and is hell bent on keeping those secrets from Faye. As the two begin to be together, they also happen along a homeless child who shows signs of abuse and together they begin their mission to find and care for the young boy. <br /><br />This story had everything I love in a novel; dimensional characters, a community feel, drama, angst and a whole boat load of romance and passion. This story (and series) is one of complete dramatics but the plot is woven together spectacularly and it's impossible not to relate to the characters, even if you have nothing in common.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/375192487?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Splage" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Splage" href="/user/show/4755656-splage">Splage</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=kidnapping">kidnapping</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=hero-heroine-virgin-innocent">hero-heroine-virgin-innocent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=epilogue-totally-fab">epilogue-totally-fab</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=in-love-with-hero-since-young">in-love-with-hero-since-young</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=sex-medium-to-very-sexy">sex-medium-to-very-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=2012-read">2012-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=alpha">alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=small-town-usa">small-town-usa</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=emotional-made-me-cry-lump-in-thr">emotional-made-me-cry-lump-in-thr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer375192487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3159338965428620002">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>5 Fraking Fantastic Stars</b><br/><br/>Angels deserve heroes and heroes deserve angels. So true, so true... Faye and Chase were each other’s destinies and I loved reading their story!<br/><br/>I had big anticipation for <b>Breathe</b> because the Colorado Mountain series is what really started me on my Kristen Ashley crazy reading obsession. I had read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_' title='Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick</a> years ago when it first came out. I loved it and KA’s style, but she didn’t have any other books published at the time. It see</span>
  <span id="freeText3159338965428620002" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>5 Fraking Fantastic Stars</b><br /><br />Angels deserve heroes and heroes deserve angels. So true, so true... Faye and Chase were each other’s destinies and I loved reading their story!<br /><br />I had big anticipation for <b>Breathe</b> because the Colorado Mountain series is what really started me on my Kristen Ashley crazy reading obsession. I had read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_" title="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a> years ago when it first came out. I loved it and KA’s style, but she didn’t have any other books published at the time. It seems now I can hardly get through a week with out reading or rereading a KA story to get my fix. <br /><br />Her typical elements were all there. It started with a bang, Chace had his share of A-hole moments to get my juices flowing and it had a hot, stirring romance between a virgin and a broken cop. The courtship was very arousing because of Faye’s inexperience and Chace’s he-man qualities in the bedroom. I still blush occasionally when KA writes her sex descriptions and dialog. Sometimes Chace’s choice of words were shockingly direct and made me flinch…in a good way.<br /><br />Faye has to be one of my favorite KA heroines. She was innocent, vulnerable and sweet; family oriented, dedicated and such a big, fat LIAR! I loved her backbone! Faye had a brand of quiet that was strong and fierce and boy, could she grandstand when she got pissed. A couple of scenes I was cheering her on, thinking you go girl! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ A phenomenal break up scene and the city council meeting come to mind. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She went all Clint Eastwood, I could just hear, “Go ahead, make my day” coming from her sweet, little librarian mouth. All the girls were back from the previous stories helping Faye get her man. Also the best was a lesbian giving <i>man</i> dating advice, how profound. Let me say, Twyla’s advice was right on…”how to unf**k a man, f**k him.” Simple and (un)sweet, gotta love it.<br /><br />There was a murder mystery to solve which was introduce in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12958487.Lady_Luck__Colorado_Mountain___3_" title="Lady Luck (Colorado Mountain, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Luck</a>. This was my only slight criticism because I didn’t really care about it. There wasn’t a huge plot development or new information to make me overly concerned. I think mainly it lacked my interest because there was another side story that overshadowed it so greatly. Malachi/Miah was a homeless boy that totally stole the show. His story had me holding my breath with anticipation. His life was harsh and brutal and I was so into finding out about this fierce, broken boy that my focus was completely surrounding his circumstances. He brought out my emotions several times. It was heartbreaking, but yet beautiful in how Chace, Faye and her family took care of him.<br /><br />The story was also about Chace’s evolution. He had a lot to overcome from the ending in <b>Lady Luck</b>, going from bad cop, worse husband to hero. I knew eventually all those wonderful attributes I have to have in my heroes; possessive, confident, protective, as well as, gorgeous, sexy, and all alpha, would reveal themselves in Chace. <br /><br />So yes, the story structure was familiar, with amazing characters, mystery and violence, and at times the hero’s crude dialog was present, but “if it ain’t broke don’t fix it” is my motto. You won’t be disappointed if you are a fan of Kristen Ashley, with her alpha heroes and her style of writing.<br /><br />KA did a great job in tying everything together so perfectly from beginning to end. I don’t want to elaborate too much because I would have to reveal some big spoilers and connections, but lets just say they were big and they made all my insides warm and my smile huge.<br /><br />The epilogue was so precious and just how I like my endings. It was like the energizer bunny…it kept going and going and giving and giving until my satisfaction was guaranteed. I mean let’s face it, I never want a KA book to end, I am too in love with the characters so it was perfect for me to have a gazillion happy endings.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3159338965428620002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_363721792" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/363721792" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/363721792?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA fangirls</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cop-hero">cop-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shy-heroine">shy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=small-town-romance">small-town-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer363721792" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10181628669000283658">Another sterling contemporary romance from Kristen Ashley – we’re back in Carnal for the story of Chace and Faye. This is one of my favourite plot lines – the tough, protective alpha hero with the sweet and really rather geeky heroine.<br/><br/>There’s a heartbreaking tale at the centre of this story about a homeless child, Malachi, living rough on the streets of Carnal and his plight is the driving force that brings Chace and Faye together. Malachi’s story will tug at your heart strings and helping him a</span>
  <span id="freeText10181628669000283658" style="display:none">Another sterling contemporary romance from Kristen Ashley – we’re back in Carnal for the story of Chace and Faye. This is one of my favourite plot lines – the tough, protective alpha hero with the sweet and really rather geeky heroine.<br /><br />There’s a heartbreaking tale at the centre of this story about a homeless child, Malachi, living rough on the streets of Carnal and his plight is the driving force that brings Chace and Faye together. Malachi’s story will tug at your heart strings and helping him allows Chace and Faye’s caring natures to really shine through.<br /><br />So, Chace. He’s absolutely typical KA hero material. He’s bossy, domineering, given to outbursts of jerk like behaviour, protective, caring and super hot – everything we’ve come to expect in a KA hero. He’s had a lot to contend with in his life so far – everyone who should have been there for him, has not been and people have taken advantage of his loyalty. He considers himself tainted by association with ‘dirty cops’, a storyline from Lady Luck, and is suffering from a serious dose of low self-esteem.<br /><br />Enter stage left – Faye Goodknight. Never was a heroine more aptly named. She may be the heroine of the novel but she is the good knight in shining armour come to rescue Chace from his lack of self-worth and show him what he means to her and everyone else in Carnal. Faye is a sci-fi geek sweetheart – she’s a 29 year old virgin and, after reading her for a few pages, I realised she’s one of us!! Chances are, if you’re reading my review, that you’re a romance novel addict, always got your head in an e-reader and have a harem full to bursting of drop dead gorgeous fictional boyfriends at your disposal. This is Faye – she’s definitely one of us!!<br /><br />I really don’t know how likely a very beautiful, well-educated 29 year old virgin actually is in modern day America, but KA writes Faye well and when she finally gives up that virginity to Chace, it’s really everything you could possibly hope it would be. Rather surprisingly painless, but deeply romantic and tender. Every girl should have a guy like Chace as her first!<br /><br />Chace and Faye take a fabulous journey together – each of them growing with their love, becoming the person they always should have been. They complete each other. There is an absolutely thrilling and suspenseful climax to their story during which I could hardly breathe and, as always, a really great epilogue. Kristen Ashley really does give good epilogue! There are also several scenes with all the Colorado Mountain men together – truly a KA fangirl’s wet dream!<br /><br /><b>Things I loved </b><br /><br />Faye reading a hot sex scene and wanting to try it out with Chace afterwards. Sound familiar girls?? <br /><br />Faye’s ‘righteous’ cyber-buddy Serenity.<br /><br />All those mountain men together.<br /><br />The promise of a Graham Reece novel.<br /><br />Deck. <br /><br /><br /><b>So, why 4 stars and not 5? </b><br /><br />This may be an unpopular opinion, but I felt I'd met Chace before - he's extremely similar and possibly interchangeable with several other KA heroes we've read before. Also, some of the sentences are overlong, especially speeches given by the central characters and I think some more stringent editing would probably improve these books.<br /><br /><br />But, it's still a fabulous KA romance, very much in her usual style.<br /><br /><br /><br />4 stars contemporary romance.<br /><br />If you enjoyed Breathe, don't forget to vote for it on the Best Kristen Ashley Books List.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/list/show/21456.Best_Kristen_Ashley_Books">http://www.goodreads.com/list/show/21...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10181628669000283658" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7312467342281819682" style="display:none"><b>Re-read for the 3rd time. Breathe kept me company during my first half-marathon! </b><br /><br />4.5 Stars of Kristen Ashley awesome! <br /><br />I loved Faye! She was a cute and funny librarian, science fiction aficionado, with a little bit of a temper to match her red hair. I cracked up every time she used that backbone and said "frak", even if she felt a little guilty saying it, like it was an actual curse word. Lol! <br /><br />I swooned hard for Chace! What a complete and total sweetheart! He melted my heart with the way he treated Faye as the most precious thing ever to grace his life. <br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><b><i><blockquote><br />"There's a temperament behind that hair, son. So, my advice, don't catch it from Faye."</blockquote><br /><br /><br /><blockquote>He wanted her for years not having any f**king clue how much of her there was to get, how deep it ran or how sweet it was.</blockquote><br /><br /><br />"Decided with one look at you, I'd put up with it, all the shit that was gettin' worse at work 'cause my end game would be you." <br /></i>Was he saying what I thought he was saying?<i> <br />"The town's sweet, cute, quiet, pretty librarian in my bed, my ring on her finger, enjoyin' it as I taught her how to enjoy it, plantin' my babies in her, building a family." <br /></i>Holy fraking frak!<i><br /><br /><blockquote>“You gonna jump on-line and tell your geek squad you landed me?” </blockquote><br /><br /><br /><blockquote>"Christ, here we go. Backbone."</blockquote></i></b><br /><br /><br />Love Kristen Ashley!<br /></span>

<div id="review_364373715" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/364373715" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/364373715?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=2012-favourites">2012-favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer364373715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2398834992086756145">For full review please go to: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/><br/><b>"Love, Drama, Salvation, Suspense, it was Dark & Horrific at times"</b><br/><br/>I have to say that for me this book was about Chase...this journey was his. To find love and happiness and redemption.<br/><br/>I slowly fell in love with Chase...not instant but the one that simmers in the background and then blows up in your face and you realize what an amazing man this is. Yes he is a hot alpha, but I didn't get him as a person...that is until his relationship w</span>
  <span id="freeText2398834992086756145" style="display:none">For full review please go to: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br /><br /><br /><b>"Love, Drama, Salvation, Suspense, it was Dark &amp; Horrific at times"</b><br /><br />I have to say that for me this book was about Chase...this journey was his. To find love and happiness and redemption.<br /><br />I slowly fell in love with Chase...not instant but the one that simmers in the background and then blows up in your face and you realize what an amazing man this is. Yes he is a hot alpha, but I didn't get him as a person...that is until his relationship with Faye unravelled. In the end I felt for him how I feel for Lawson...this decent, honourable man who's all about what is right, respect, love and devotion. Protecting what's his what he sees as important. He doesn't see himself in the right light, he has had a lonely life, dictated by others but not in a positive way which means he paints himself with the same brush. He can't take himself out of the equation, believing he is like them not by actions but by default. In Faye it's almost like he sees redemption. He sees her as innocent, vulnerable and adorable and his attraction has been there years but it's almost like he is scared to taint her with his ugliness! To him she truly is an Angel; unspoilt.<br /><br /><i>"He’d been touched by the hand of an angel" - Chase<br /><br />“You in my life, me livin’ in hell, feels like I’ve been touched by an angel.” - Chase<br /><br />"Then he said quietly in my ear, “For a long time, a long fuckin’ time, Faye, nearly six years, I thought it was certain I’d never have anything as beautiful as the last three minutes. Thank you, honey, for giving that to me.”</i> - Chase<br /><br />All he wants is a family, a wife he loves and loves him in return, kids. A happy home..he wants affection! Chace is in awe of Faye's family..it's his dream to be part of his own, by his making! He realises what he could have had, the regrets, the wasted years.<br /><br /><i>"He’d wanted her for years not having any fucking clue how much of her there was to get, how deep it ran or how sweet it was"</i> - Chase .. I loved this sentence it says it ALL!!<br /><br />He is so loving, and has this vulnerable side to him. He values Faye for who she is and what she has become to him and it shows when he safe guards Faye's 'innocence' and guides her with this amazing protective hand. At the same time he revels in the fact that this is a gift for him, one that has never been given to anyone else one he knows it is his alone. <br /><br /><i>"I’m falling for you... But you know that since you know I already did it thirteen years ago. I held out for a hero"</i> - Faye<br /><br />He isn't scared to show Faye his emotions a testament to how he feels about her and how she acts towards him...he feels safe in doing so. When she gave him her, he knew what this meant!<br /><br /><i>"A taste of sweet.<br />The touch of an angel.<br />A trace of a miracle"</i> - Chase<br /><br />Chace is beyond a hero, although he doesn't see himself this way. His protection of Malachi, his fight for what's right. My heart melted... it broke me. The true amazing trait of any man....not only the kind of hero Faye meant but the ultimate hero by actions and the sense of right and his non questioning protection. He thinks he is lost, changed...soiled by the past wanting to redeem himself. He has no clue how amazing he is. He is given a test to save Faye and it was heart stopping. To him, I think this moment, he found his own salvation from the sins of others.<br /><br /><i>“Baby,” Chace whispered...... “Breathe.”</i> - I forgot how to at times!<br /><br />Now Faye. I absolutely loved Faye. I identified with so many aspects of her character. The quiet shy girl with her nose in a book. But really underneath the 'superficial' is a woman who knows who she is, she is fierce, strong, grounded, extremely funny, adorable and vulnerable. She knows life can deal you bad situation and she is not naive or ignorant to the fact of real life. She reads to escape for moments of dreams and fantasy. Yet she knows all that goes on and she is fully aware of Chace and his situation. She has been in love with Chase for 13 years, solid in her belief that he is the one for her. Such conviction, such perseverance. Her unwavering loyalty, devotion and love for this man means that she is adamant she will set him free, heal what is broken, seek justice for her man,. This despite the fact that he isn't so yet. And despite knowing he maybe never be she shows her true selflessness through pure emotion and adoration.<br />She is in awe of him, truly devoted, yet she does not stand down or let him intimidate her into a situation she does not agree with. I admired her for not letting him go. She stood firm, she didn't let the wanting of him overshadow what was ultimately right for her. This is also despite knowing that Chase has NEVER had anyone look out for him before with such love and protection, she took a gamble, a risk for him to understand what he was being given; what he has never had!!<br /><br />Despite the pretty scary and heart breaking story line surrounding them, their journey was BEAUTIFUL!!!!<br /><br />Be prepared for some pretty special surprises too ;0)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2398834992086756145" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_371080557" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/371080557" />
    <a title="KatLynne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne"><img alt="KatLynne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296698899p2/2435483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/371080557?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KatLynne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KatLynne" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne">KatLynne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=kindle-owned">kindle-owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=one-of-my-fav-authors">one-of-my-fav-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=sensual-steamy">sensual-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong">heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=keeper">keeper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-alpha-warrior">hero-alpha-warrior</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay">hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-i-loved">heroine-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=one-of-my-favorite-series">one-of-my-favorite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer371080557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14423473464486536022"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>I need a hero; I’m holding out for a hero till the end of the night. He’s gotta be strong, he’s gotta be fast, and he’s got to be fresh from the fight. I need a hero, I’m holding out for a hero till the morning light, he’s gotta be sure, and its gotta be soon, and he’s gotta be larger than life.</b><blockquote> Faye Goodknight held out for a hero and what a remarkable one she got!</blockquote> We first meet sexy Detective Chace Keaton in Lady Luck. While being an excellent detective, he had to get dirty in his batt</span>
  <span id="freeText14423473464486536022" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>I need a hero; I’m holding out for a hero till the end of the night. He’s gotta be strong, he’s gotta be fast, and he’s got to be fresh from the fight. I need a hero, I’m holding out for a hero till the morning light, he’s gotta be sure, and its gotta be soon, and he’s gotta be larger than life.</b><blockquote> Faye Goodknight held out for a hero and what a remarkable one she got!</blockquote> We first meet sexy Detective Chace Keaton in Lady Luck. While being an excellent detective, he had to get dirty in his battle to help clear Carnal of their crew of dirty cops. Life also had smacked him with a dish that was nearly unbearable to swallow as he is forced to marry a woman he despises in order to cover the sins of a father he can barely tolerate. And even though he spent five long years avoiding everything about her, he certainly didn’t want to see her life end by a brutal murder. <blockquote> I don’t know how she does it but KA always gives me a hero I love to read about and by the end of the story, I have completely fallen for him. Chace Keaton is another sexy as sin beautiful alpha man who loves his woman, is possessive and protective. What I loved most about him was his willingness to turn his back on “everything he was” in order to protect those he loved most in this world. He was a man who would do anything to keep his loved ones safe. </blockquote><i> “He’s a white knight on a fiery steed except his steed comes in the form of an SUV and it’s not fiery. It’s burgundy.”</i> <br /><br />All he’d ever wanted was to be a good cop, have a wife, family and a home. Believing those dreams are gone forever there is a bone deep loneliness to him that is nearly tangible. He’s also a man battling demons from the residual filth of wallowing with dirty cops and feels he can never be clean again. <br /><br />What he needed was one of the best heroines in this series, Faye Goodknight. Twenty-nine years old, she has loved him since a teenager. She’s the local librarian and while shy, this lady has backbone. She’s smart, warm, compassionate and somewhat geeky with her nose always in a book. She is perfect for Chace and without a doubt his knight! As this passionate love story unfolds, he soon learns for the first time in his life what it feels like to have someone at his back, loving him and teaching him he couldn’t shoulder the world’s burdens and he didn’t have to. She was his angel, He was her hero. <blockquote>
  <i> “Twenty-nine years, I held out for this. Then, half an hour later, you proved every one of these words true and every moment since then, you kept doing it. I’ll take you thinking I’m your angel but you need to know you’re my hero. Twenty-nine, honey, I held out for this. Twenty-nine years, I held out for you.”</i>
</blockquote> This book was everything and more; a passionate, poignant love story that left me breathless many times. A man desperately needing deliverance and acceptance and quickly realizes he needs his angel in order to breathe. And a young woman who is so lonely for her hero, a true damsel in distress and one who’s knight certainly doesn’t fail! <blockquote>
  <i> “I'll let you in on a secret, honey. The knight who has serious chinks in his armor but never falls is the true hero. That means he's won battles and doesn't waste time polishing his armor so he can be good while he rides in parades that are tributes to his glory. He just drags himself back on his steed and keeps right on battling. And if he's the right kind of knight, he never rides alone. The best heroes inspire loyalty. The best heroes keep fighting the good fight, tirelessly, quietly. The best heroes always have scars. If they didn't, the heroine would have nothing to do. It's her job to help the hero let all that stuff go in order that her man can be strong enough to fight on but when he's with her he's free to just 'breathe'.” </i>
</blockquote>Kristen Ashley is a captivating story teller who knows how to add all the right ingredients to create a page turner that you don’t want to put down. It pulled my heart in all the right places and is another favorite to add to my keeper shelf.<br /><br />As always, she gives us a cast of secondary characters that enhances the enjoyment of the story along with villains you despise. From early on is the mystery of a young homeless boy, Malachi. Without giving anything away, all I will say is to have plenty of tissues on hand as this young child’s story is heartbreaking and will grab you and pull hard on your heartstrings. <br /><br />An added highlight was visiting once again with those characters I have come to love in Carnal and Gnaw Bone and catching up on all their news! There is a pregnancy and birth along with a very delightful surprise. I really enjoyed how KA incorporated this well known character into the life of Faye! And let’s not forget her stellar Epilogue!<br /><br /><i>Breathe,</i> so aptly named as I found myself quite breathless with many of the moving scenes and with one in particular holding my breath anxiously, almost forgetting to breathe myself!<br /><br />I couldn’t help but include one of Faye’s songs in this review. It’s beautiful; it’s one of her favorites and plays an integral part in her life. Ella Mae Bowen’s <i> “Holding Out for A Hero” </i><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QoWSf_QFfi8">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QoWSf_...</a><br /><br />And for me, Jason Mraz’s <i> “I Want Give Up”</i> kept playing in my head and I gave this one to Chase:)<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XLOMvPC1EzQ">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XLOMvP...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14423473464486536022" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_379077720" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/379077720" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/379077720?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15767003-breathe">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone who loves a good emotional romance.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2013_reads">2013_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer379077720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3367953311033671539">So....10,00+ ratings, <b>801</b> reviews(!), <i>what can I add that hasn't already been said</i>? In the words of 29-year-old virgin heroine Faye Goodnight...<b>
  <i>"Um..."</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>I loved this book.</b> Probably my favorite (at least the characters were my favorites) of all the KA books I've read so far. I'll admit at first I thought 35-year-old police detective Chace Keaton was incredibly rude to our heroine Faye, especially when he told her to "move her fat ass". But I get it, all KA's heroes have to have at least one mom</span>
  <span id="freeText3367953311033671539" style="display:none">So....10,00+ ratings, <b>801</b> reviews(!), <i>what can I add that hasn't already been said</i>? In the words of 29-year-old virgin heroine Faye Goodnight...<b>
  <i>"Um..."</i>
</b><br><br><b>I loved this book.</b> Probably my favorite (at least the characters were my favorites) of all the KA books I've read so far. I'll admit at first I thought 35-year-old police detective Chace Keaton was incredibly rude to our heroine Faye, especially when he told her to "move her fat ass". But I get it, all KA's heroes have to have at least one moment of asshat behavior, and he did make it up to her (*sigh*) many, many times. So all is forgiven.<br><br><i>Chace...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr013/68db3d24-1ce4-40c3-b4a5-1aa2180c91dc_zpsba7b3354.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385657i/744694.jpg" alt=" photo 68db3d24-1ce4-40c3-b4a5-1aa2180c91dc_zpsba7b3354.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I loved that KA made Faye a "geek". A beautiful geek, but a geek nonetheless. Totally relatable. Town librarian, fan of geeky television, always with her nose in a book, geeky online friends, <i>and</i> a 29-year-old virgin who's been crushing on our hero (she's been "holding out for a hero") for <i>13 years</i>! And she thinks he hasn't noticed her just because they've never spoken in all that time...<br><br><i>Faye...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr013/8fa3dbae-5e8d-46c5-b023-804d5c599847_zps00c2a036.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385657i/744695.jpg" alt=" photo 8fa3dbae-5e8d-46c5-b023-804d5c599847_zps00c2a036.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm not going into the plot--the book blurb handles that well. I liked how Faye and Chace finally got together, how they bonded over their quest to help a little abused boy (Miah). We see that both Faye and Chace have kind hearts and work hard to correct a wrong that has been done.<br><br>I got completely immersed in this one. Everything about it was just fantastic. The leads, the plot, the touch of suspense, the sex scenes (and there were many), the supporting players--all perfect. Never was I tempted to skip a page (and KA provided many, many details that could've been edited for a faster moving story--but I really liked reading every single non-essential detail!) Chace and Faye's romance was red hot, romantic, and sinfully sensual. I truly believed that these two had fallen in love--and <i>I loved it!</i> Intensely romantic <i>and</i> erotic.:)<br><br>This book made me tear up at the oddest moments. When Miah called Chace his "Aslan"...I could feel the tears flowing...<br><br><i>Wise, compassionate, powerful Aslan...</i>just like Chace<br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr001/aslan_zpse8c713cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385657i/744696.jpg" alt=" photo aslan_zpse8c713cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved Chace.<br>I loved Faye.<br>I loved them together.<br>And I especially loved that awesome epilogue! Thank you KA for not leaving the reader hanging and wondering.<br><br>It's been a few days since I finished this one and I'm having a hard time moving on. I felt the same way about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17257993.Raid__Unfinished_Hero___3_" title="Raid (Unfinished Hero, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Raid</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13640229.Creed__Unfinished_Hero___2_" title="Creed (Unfinished Hero, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Creed</a>. KA is a fantastic storyteller but her books take an emotional toll on me! 5 stars<br><br><i>Warning: This book contains explicit sex, including oral, and some heartbreaking subject matter about child abuse. Not for sensitive readers.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3367953311033671539" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
