<div id="review_377791455" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/377791455" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/377791455?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer377791455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13339031077250260042"><i>
  <b>"I need a hero<br/>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br/>He's gotta be strong, he's gotta be fast<br/>And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br/>I need a hero<br/>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br/>He's gotta be sure, he's gotta be soon<br/>And he's gotta be larger than life, larger than life."</b>
</i> -- <b>Holding Out For A Hero by Ella Mae Bowen.</b><br/><br/>God, what to say. I don't know where to start. <br/><br/>I guess, I'll begin with...<br/><br/><b>THIS IS MY MOST FAV KA READ I'VE EVER HAD THE PLEASURE OF READING.</b><br/><br/>Yes, my most </span>
  <span id="freeText13339031077250260042" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I need a hero<br />I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br />He's gotta be strong, he's gotta be fast<br />And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br />I need a hero<br />I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br />He's gotta be sure, he's gotta be soon<br />And he's gotta be larger than life, larger than life."</b>
</i> -- <b>Holding Out For A Hero by Ella Mae Bowen.</b><br /><br />God, what to say. I don't know where to start. <br /><br />I guess, I'll begin with...<br /><br /><b>THIS IS MY MOST FAV KA READ I'VE EVER HAD THE PLEASURE OF READING.</b><br /><br />Yes, my most <b>FAV</b> read <b>EVER.</b> Chace took Tack's place, he ran over Callum. I'm not sure how it happened. It caught me off guard. I was not expecting to love him the way I do. He started off as the worlds worst asshole, and somewhere between a dance in Faye's bedroom and a kiss against the Library wall, I fell. I fell so deep, I drowned. And I'm still drowning. <br /><br />Chace. This man, he's become my everything. So misunderstood. He's fathers a douche, his mother, mentally unstable. He was pushed into a marriage he never wanted and then his wife was murdered. I really felt like his spirit was smothered and as Ella Bowen says, he's "fresh from the fight." So raw, so wounded, carrying the wait of the world on his beautiful shoulders and all the while, he's yearning for the town's sweet, shy and precious librarian. A girl who makes him feel clean, like he's tasted the sweetest thing he'll ever taste in all his life. <br /><br />God. I'm crying again. He makes me cry. He makes me sob. He's such a brilliant man, you guys. He's a <b>REAL</b> man. A man who makes me breathless and so very mushy inside. I'm in love with him. With everything he is. I can't put it into words. I'm trying, but there's nothing. This is the type of man who you want to wrap yourself around and never let go. He's protective, possessive. He cares about family. All he's ever wanted was to do right in the world, marry a girl, give her babies, take care of his kids, while living in a big house, on acres of land with a white picket fence. <br /><br />It's magical! AHHHHHHHH!<br /><br />And while he is a <b>GOOD</b> man, he still maintains an alpha streak that makes you weak in the knees. <br /><br />Jesus, I feel him. I feel him <b>BIG TIME!</b><br /><br />Faye. Sweet. Gentle. I <b>LOVED</b> her. She's a dreamer, always has her head in the clouds. And she's been holding out for a hero and that hero is, Chace Keaton. <b>OMG. OMG. OMG.</b> I can't say enough about this girl. She's me. Nerdy, a bookworm. But she has such a huge heart. <br /><br />Goodness. These characters overwhelm me. Just thinking of them takes my breath away. <br /><br />I really <b>LOVED</b> this book. Typical with Kristen Ashley books there is drama, and angst, but there's also a soothing balm in place. Moments of comedic relief that help you get through the tough feels. And there were some really tough moments in this book. <br /><br /><b>I CRIED. <br />AND I CRIED. <br />AND THEN I CRIED. <br /><br />SHIT, I CRIED DURING SEX.<br />SEX!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! </b><br /><br />Hahahahahaha! There was so much emotion in this book. It's something I cannot explain, but as I kept reading, I kept listening to this song...<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I need a hero<br />I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br />He's gotta be strong, he's gotta be fast<br />And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br />I need a hero<br />I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br />He's gotta be sure, he's gotta be soon<br />And he's gotta be larger than life, larger than life.</i>
</b><br /><br />And with every word, my heart beat faster for these two characters. I, too, am a dreamer. So I really related to Faye and I fell in love with her as she fell in love. <br /><br />Between Chace, Miah and Becky, Faye's family and just the entire cast of characters this book became and all time <b>FAVORITE</b>. I'll never forget a minute of it. <b>NEVER.</b> <br /><br />A <b>PHENOMENAL</b> journey that I'm completely hungover from. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13339031077250260042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1590143444" />
    <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review"><img alt="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465424458p2/44132489.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1590143444?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20494223-breathe">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=nerdy-or-quirky">nerdy-or-quirky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=protective-alpha">protective-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1590143444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11614825468130273060">I'm really enjoying this series. The hero jerk moments are on the low end for KA books, and thank goodness because some of those bad moments can ruin a book for me. <br/><br/>In Chase's case he was trying to protect Faye. His jerkiness also didn't last long. Once Chase decided he couldn't stay away from her, these two were just adorable together. I really enjoyed seeing the town's hunky cop pursuing the town's shy librarian. <br/><br/>Faye was cute. She was a total geek and she came off as a very sweet person with </span>
  <span id="freeText11614825468130273060" style="display:none">I'm really enjoying this series. The hero jerk moments are on the low end for KA books, and thank goodness because some of those bad moments can ruin a book for me. <br /><br />In Chase's case he was trying to protect Faye. His jerkiness also didn't last long. Once Chase decided he couldn't stay away from her, these two were just adorable together. I really enjoyed seeing the town's hunky cop pursuing the town's shy librarian. <br /><br />Faye was cute. She was a total geek and she came off as a very sweet person with a bit of a temper. That temper saved her from being a stale character. The only thing I didn't enjoy was her constant use of the word Frak in place of the F word. It was used a lot. <br /><br />I love that we got to see the same side characters again. Their loyalty and friendship really adds a lot to the couples story. I loved that we got more closure to the town's criminal activity that was happening in the previous books, and last but not least, I also enjoyed the storyline with the homeless boy. Got me right in the heart.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11614825468130273060" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_639130892" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639130892" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639130892?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17755575-wendy-sthoughts?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639130892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer872726835431816674"><b>5 Her Hero Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>I have been re-reading the Colorado series and Breathe has always been a true favorite. There was just something that drew me in… Faye Goodknight, this sweet, shy, smart librarian, who was a home grown gal devoted to her town and family had the ability to see the good in Chace Keaton, a man tortured by his past actions which had been thrust upon him. Kristen Ashley coupled a sexually inexperienced woman with a pure, full-fledged, long time, pining love for t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText872726835431816674" style="display:none"><b>5 Her Hero Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>I have been re-reading the Colorado series and Breathe has always been a true favorite. There was just something that drew me in… Faye Goodknight, this sweet, shy, smart librarian, who was a home grown gal devoted to her town and family had the ability to see the good in Chace Keaton, a man tortured by his past actions which had been thrust upon him. Kristen Ashley coupled a sexually inexperienced woman with a pure, full-fledged, long time, pining love for the confident, heroic, Alpha cop. It was a combination to set the heart a flutter.<br><br>Ashley layered this with so many variables; Faye may have been inexperienced in actions but had a vision of what “her man” should be. She had been reading romance for ages and knew what character traits she wanted. <br><br>She even had a personal theme song. The slower, countrified Ella Mae Bowen’s version of Holding Out For A Hero. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3FnOY86v390">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3FnOY...</a></b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Where have all the good men gone<br>And where are all the gods?<br>Where's the street-wise Hercules<br>To fight the rising odds?<br>Isn't there a white knight upon a fiery steed?<br>Late at night I toss and turn and dream of what I need<br><br>I need a hero<br>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br>He's gotta be strong, he's gotta be fast<br>And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br>I need a hero<br>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br>He's gotta be sure, he's gotta be soon<br>And he's gotta be larger than life, larger than life<br><br>Somewhere after midnight<br>In my wildest fantasies<br>Somewhere just beyond my reach<br>There's someone reaching back for me<br>Racing on the thunder and rising with the heat<br>Isn't there a superman to sweep me off my feet?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Her family was loving and hardworking. She also had perfect role models with her mom and dad. This was a man who wouldn't watch and let a wrong go by without standing up and fighting against it. He taught her through his actions and words that to watch something unjust happen and not do something to right it was morally equal to the one doing the wrong. <br><br>Faye did not live in a vacuum, she was aware of all the corruption her town has gone through…watching the pain her personal hero had thrust on him. Now the town was lauding him as a savior and he wanted nothing of it….it was just an additional weight to carry. <br><br>Chace Keaton was living a nightmare.<br><br>From the first understanding of what his family was, Chace knew he needed to follow another path then the one expected of him. He came from Big Money... His father was a Mover and Shaker who had very clear ideas of what Chace should do and be... an extension of the corrupt power his father held. The only sweetness Chace experienced growing up was from his mother.... though she was what the moneied would call <i>Delicate</i>. Chace learned what would set his mother off and it was mostly his father. <br><br>Chace decided early on to not be his father's puppet and left home at 18 never looking back. He became a cop of the small town of Carnal, a far cry from Aspen. There he was his own man and able to live a life where he knew he would be free to find what he wanted....<br><br>And what he wanted more than anything was the sweet, shy, smart librarian, Faye Goodknight. He saw her and thought, when he was ready... she was who he wanted for a lifetime...He just needed to make his play and everything would fall into place...<br><br>But life doesn't always follow our plans, and Chace got caught up in the web of corruption and deceit the Carnal police department was trapped under the charge of a dirty chief. Chace stood strong and balanced a line he drew in the sand...He tried to stay true to himself...but then things became so filthy... he had to make decisions that changed both his life and Faye's...<br><br>Now the town has been saved and thinks Chace's involvement makes him a hero...something he knows he doesn't deserve...It is a weight and feeling he cannot let go of...It also makes him feel he will never be clean enough to deserve a sweet woman like Faye. <br><br>But...Chace never expected Faye to stand, confront him and show him the way to her. He knows he shouldn't get involved with her...but the pull is just too much and he finally gives into what his heart wants...<br><br>Ashley gives us a story with layers of learning to be who you are, what you are able to be and the necessity of forgiving yourself from things that happened in the past....She shows there are other perspectives that may see things differently... and to be willing to share and be let things go...<br><br>She also takes a woman who has a vision of life...who has held out for a love she thought never would happen... and takes it with gusto...Faye is all in and Chace has a way with her that is sweet, strong and sometimes manipulative...but when Faye feels it is time to dig in and say her piece, she is a wonder... Her strength and beliefs are everything. She is woman to be proud of...<br><br>The romance elements with this is sweet and hot all at the same time. These two burn so hot for each other... and she is putty in his hands...As he is instinctively aware of her inexperience, he takes this responsibility seriously and makes baby steps along the way until both are more than ready to take the relationship forward. Sexy times are intense and we are in both Faye and Chace's heads as they are exploring their feelings....Yum.<br><br>As with all Ashley books, there is also a meaty plot of things involving our couple. More suspense and concern. We get to have all the other Carnal characters we love from past books to interact with Faye and Chace. Everything fit and made me wish for more....<br><br>And since I am doing a re-read, I knew more was coming. Ashley proceed to re-visit the Colorado Series with three more books, Jagged in 2013, Kaleidoscope in 2014 and Bounty in 2016. Although these last books each have their own charm...for me, the first four books have always been the heart of the series. <br><br><b>
  <i> 3/2018-<br>I went on a Kristen Ashley Binge in 2013. I recently re-read The Gamble and it put me in the mood to do all of the Colorado Mountain Series...one of my favorite of hers. Since I was very new to Goodreads, I never dreamt of reviewing. <br><br>When I finish, I will be reviewing this time. </i>
</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327890208s/11227041.jpg" alt="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QZtW7efv94hWa0ta/9ckJZpEDMWEIfM/JABgWOccp5VPafBrw9uvMBPer5TNOFm2eSMS7dwd9F4zDZGBNI6TZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BPThPSM8NQ8u9NGYpDV0KF8y7Tma7r1awqY2zR5NKZsKBke7Bwhtt2tBNVaW2gm7vFXzEcLSujvVq8cUzd8daA==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText8191222349812174061" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/21429192-breathe">Quotes from Breathe</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;<i>I'll let you in on a secret, honey. The knight who has serious chinks in his armor but never falls is the true hero. That means he's won battles and doesn't waste time polishing his armor so he can look good while he rides in parades that are tributes to his glory. He just drags himself back on his steed and keeps right on battling. And if he's the right kind of knight, he never rides alone. The best heroes inspire loyalty. The best heroes keep fighting the good fight, tirelessly, quietly. The best heroes always have scars. If they didn't, the heroine would have nothing to do. It's her job to help the hero let all that stuff go in order that her man can be strong enough to fight on but when he's with her he's free to just 'breathe'.<i></i></i>&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/594982-i-ll-let-you-in-on-a-secret-honey-the-knight">188 likes</a>
